varuṇasya vai suṣuvāṇasya bhargo apākrāmat sa tredhāpatad bhṛgus tṛtīyam abhavac chrāyantīyaṃ tṛtīyam apas tṛtīyaṃ prāviśat yad bhārgavo hotā bhavati tenaiva tad indriyaṃ vīryam āptvāvarundhe yat śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad indriyaṃ vīryam āptvārundhe yat puṣkarasrajaṃ pratimuñcate tenaiva tad indriyaṃ vīryam āptvāvarundhe daśamī bhavati daśa camasā daśa camasādhvaryavo daśa daśa camasam abhiyanty ā daśamāt puruṣād anvākhyāya prasarpanti daśa samṛddho hy eṣa yajña enaṃ vāva te tad yajñam anvaicchan ya etena yajata etad evendriyaṃ vīryam āttvāsmin dadhāti sarvaḥ saptadaśo bhavati dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavaḥ sa vai saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsarād evendriyaṃ vīryam āptvāvarundhe indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasyeyaṃ citrāṇy upaid rūpāṇy asau nakṣatrāṇām avakāśena puṇḍarīkaṃ jāyate yat puṣkarasrajaṃ pratimuñcate vṛtrasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kṣatraṃ pratimuñcate dvādaśa puṣkarā bhavanti dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsare antar bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca bhūtena caivainaṃ bhavyena ca samardhayati srag udgātus saurya udgātā na vai tasmai vyaucchad atho vy evāsmai vāsayati rukmo hotur āgneyo hotātho amum evāsmā ādityam unnayati prākāśāv adhvaryor yāv iva hy adhvaryū atho cakṣuṣī evāsmin dadhāti aśvaḥ prastotuḥ prājāpatyo aśvaḥ prājāpatyaḥ prastotātho preva hy aśvaḥ prothati preva prastotā stauti dhenuḥ pratihartuḥ paya evāsmin dadhāti vaśā maitrāvaruṇasya vaśaṃ mā nayād iti ṛṣabho brāhmaṇācchaṃsino vīryaṃ vā ṛṣabho vīryam evāsmin dadhāti vāsaḥ potuḥ pavitratvāya varāsī neṣṭur anulambeva hy eṣā hotrā sthūri yavācitam acchāvākasya sthūrir iva hy eṣā hotrātho nirvaruṇatvāyaiva yavā na vai tarhi yad asyāṃ dakṣiṇā abhy abhavann atho asya ta eva tenābhīṣṭāḥ prītā bhavanti anaḍvān agnīdho yuktyai ajaḥ subrahmaṇyāyai vatsatary unnetuḥ sāṇḍas trivatso grāvastuto mithunatvāya dvādaśa paṣṭhauhyo garbhiṇyo brahmaṇo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhaty atha yad garbhiṇyo vāg vai dhenur mantro garbho vācy evāsya mantraṃ dadhāty āmantraṇīyo bhavaty atha yad dhenubhavyā dvādaśa payāṃsi tāny evāsmin dadhāti tasmād āhuḥ payasvī rājā puṇya iti

yo vai savād eti nainaṃ sava upanamaty atha yaḥ sāmabhya eti pāpīyān suṣuvāṇo bhavati saṃbhāryā bhavanti pṛṣṭhāny eva tābhir yunakti etāni vāva sāmāni yat pṛṣṭhāni yat saṃbhāryā bhavanti tad eva sāmabhyo naiti yāni devarājñāṃ sāmāni tair amuṣmin loka ṛdhnoti yāni manuṣyarājñāṃ tair asminn ubhayor anayor lokayor ṛdhnoti devaloke ca manuṣyaloke ca sāmatriṣṭubhy adhy abhiṣicyate vīryaṃ vai sāma triṣṭup vīrya evādhy abhiṣicyate ekādaśa rājasāmāni bhavanty ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasy eva vīrye adhy abhiṣicyate yat trivṛtam abhiṣecanīye kuryur brahma kṣatrāyāpidadhyur yat trivṛtam uddharanti brahma tat kṣatrād uddharanti tasmād bharatāṃ pratidaṇḍā brahmaṇā na hi te trivṛtam abhiṣecanīye kurvanti ekaviṃśo abhiṣecanīyasyottamaḥ saptadaśo daśapeya ekaviṃśaḥ keśavapanīyasya prathamaḥ kṣatraṃ vā ekaviṃśo viṭ saptadaśaḥ kṣatreṇaivāsmai viśam ubhayataḥ parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viṭ bhavati yad vai rājasūyenābhiṣicyate tat svargaṃ lokam ārohati sa yad imaṃ lokaṃ nopāvarohed ati janaṃ vā gacched ud vā mādyed yad eṣo arvācīnastomaḥ keśavapanīyo bhavaty asya lokasyānuddhānāya yathā śākhāyāḥ śākhām ālambham upāvarohed evam etenemaṃ lokam upāvarohati pratiṣṭhāyai

indro vṛtram ahan sa viṣyaṅvīryeṇa vyabhraṃśata sa etac chrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇād indriyeṇa vā eṣa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyate yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate vṛtraṃ hi hanti yac chrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi bhavati vācā vā eṣa vyṛdhyate yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate vṛtraṃ hi hanti vāg anuṣṭub vāco raso yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāsya rasaṃ dadhāti vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavatīndriyeṇa vā eṣa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyate yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate vṛtraṃ hi hanti yad vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavatīndriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai aśrayan vāva śrāyantīyenāvārayanta vāravantīyenendriyasya vā eṣā vīryasya parigṛhītiḥ apratiṣṭhito vā eṣa yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate yadā vā etena dvirātreṇa yajate athaiva pratiṣṭhā yāvanti saṃvatsarasyāhorātrāṇi tāvatya etāḥ stotrīyāḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar atirātra uttaraṃ nānaivāhorātrayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati amāvāsyāyāṃ pūrvam ahar udriṣṭa [em caland uddṛṣṭa] uttaraṃ nānaivārdhamāsayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati paurṇamāsyāṃ pūrvam ahar vyaṣṭakāyām uttaraṃ nānaiva māsoḥ pratitiṣṭhati tad āhur ya eva samānapakṣe puṇyāhanī syātāṃ tayor eva kāryaṃ samṛdhyai apaśavyo dvirātra ity āhur dve hy ete chandasī gāyatraṃ ca traiṣṭubhaṃ ca jagatīm antaryantīti na tena jagatī kṛtā yat tṛtīyasavane kriyate yadā vā eṣāhīnasyāhar bhajate sāhvasya vā savanam athaiva jagatī kṛtā traiśokam uttarasyāhno brahmasāma bhavati vaikhānasam acchāvākasāma yac chukriye savane kriyete tenaiva jagatī kṛtā tena paśavyaḥ vyuṣṭir vā eṣa dvirātro vy evāsmai vāsayati

athaiṣa rāṭ yo rājya āśaṃsamāno rājyaṃ na prāpnuyāt sa etena yajeta rājaivainaṃ rājānaṃ karoti taṃ tu vairājeti vadeyur yaṃ rājā rājānaṃ kuryād rājaivainaṃ rājānaṃ karoti chando anye yajñāḥ saṃpadyante stomam eṣa vīryaṃ vai stomo vīrya evādhy abhiṣicyate aṣṭāv ekaviṃśāḥ saṃstuto bhavaty aṣṭau vai vīrā rāṣṭraṃ samudyacchanti rājabhrātā ca rājaputraś ca purohitaś ca mahiṣī ca sūtaś ca grāmaṇī ca kṣattā ca saṃgrahītā caite vai vīrā rāṣṭraṃ samudyacchanty eteṣv evādhy abhiṣicyate kṣatraṃ vā ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhā kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda

athaiṣa virāḍ annādyakāmo yajeta parokṣam anye yajñā virājaṃ saṃpadyante pratyakṣam eṣa virājaṃ saṃpannaḥ pratyakṣam etenānnādyam avarundhe annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda sarvo daśadaśī bhavati daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai tā u pañca pañca bhavanti pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktā paśavo yajña eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati etenaiva pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeta daśabhir vā idaṃ puruṣaḥ pratiṣṭhito asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati

athaiṣa aupaśadaḥ gandharvāpsarasāṃ stomaḥ prajākāmo yajeta gandharvāpsaraso vai manuṣyasya prajāyā vāprajastāyā veśate teṣām atra somapīthas tān svena bhāgadheyena prīṇāti te asmai tṛptāḥ prītāḥ prajāṃ prayacchanti ekaikā stotrīyopajāyate prajām evāsmā upajanayati kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhati puruṣo vai kakub garbha eva sa madhyato dhīyate atha yad eṣā dvipadā kakubho loke kriyate garbha eva tad dhi taṃ prajanayati cyāvanaṃ bhavati prajātir vai cyāvanam prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda vasiṣṭhasya janitre bhavato vasiṣṭho vā ete putrahataḥ sāmanī apaśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad ete sāmanī bhavataḥ prajātyai dve saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyete dve striyā ūne prajananāya prajananam eva tat kriyate prajātyai

athaiṣa punaḥstomaḥ yo bahu pratigṛhya garagīr iva manyeta sa etena yajeta yaikādaśī yad eva pūrvavayase bahu pratigṛhṇāti yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti prātaḥsavanāya tan niharati atha yā dvādaśī yad evottaravayase bahu pratigṛhṇati yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti tṛtīyasavanāya tan niharati vairājo vai puruṣaḥ sa madhyato aśuddho madhyata evainaṃ pāpmano muñcati śuddhāśuddhīye bhavataḥ indro yatīn sālāvṛkeyebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so aśuddho amanyata sa ete śuddhāśuddhīye apaśyat tābhyām aśudhyat yad eva bahu pratigṛhṇāti yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti yad aśuddho manyate tad etābhyāṃ śudhyati gauṣūktaṃ cāśvasūktaṃ ca bhavataḥ gauṣūktiś cāśvasūktiś ca bahu pratigṛhya garagirāv amanyetāṃ tāv ete sāmanī apaśyatāṃ tābhyāṃ garaṃ niraghnātām yad eva bahu pratigṛhṇāti yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti tad etābhyāṃ nirhate pañcadaśa stotrāṇi bhavanty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ pāpmana evainaṃ muktvaujasā vīryeṇa samardhayati

athaiṣa catuṣṭomaḥ paśukāmo yajeta yac catasṛbhir bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśūn evāvarundhe yad aṣṭābhir ājyāny aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti yat dvādaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāno dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ paśavo anu prajāyante tān evāvarundhe yat ṣoḍaśāni pṛṣṭhāni ṣoḍaśa kalāḥ paśavaḥ kalāśas tat paśūn āpnoti yad viṃśa ārbhavaḥ pāṅktatvam eṣāṃ tad āpnoti yac caturviṃśo agniṣṭomaś caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate ekaṃ sāma bahūni chandāṃsi tasmād eko bahūn poṣān puṣyati ātmā vā agniṣṭomaḥ paśavaś chandāṃsy ātmany eva tat paśūn pratiṣṭhāpayati noktho nāgniṣṭomo na hi grāmyāḥ paśavo nāraṇyāḥ

atha yasya catvāri stotrāṇi catasṛbhiś catvāry aṣṭābhiś catvāri dvādaśabhiś catvāri ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sa gāṃ nātivadati ṣoḍaśakalāḥ paśavaḥ kalāśas tat paśūn [kss bi praśūn] āpnoti ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśimān bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni vajraḥ ṣoḍaśī vajreṇaivāsmai paśūn parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukā asmāt paśavo bhavanti noktho nātirātro na hi grāmyāḥ paśavo nāraṇyāḥ

asurāṇāṃ vai balas tamasā prāvṛto aśmāpidhānaś cāsīt tasmin gavyaṃ vasv antar āsīt taṃ devā nāśaknuvan bhettuṃ te bṛhaspatim abruvann imān na utsṛjeti sa udbhidaiva balaṃ vyacyāvayad balabhidābhinat tān utsedhenaivodasṛjan niṣedhena paryagṛhṇāt paśukāmo yajeta yad udbhidā yajeta balam evasmai vicyāvayati yad balabhidā balam evāsmai bhinatti utsedhaniṣedhau brahmasāmanī bhavata utsedhenaivāsmai paśūn utsidhya niṣedhena parigṛhṇāti "yajña indram avardhayad" iti brahmaṇa ājyaṃ rūpeṇa samṛddham saptisaptadaśau bhavato yat saptabhiḥ stuvanti sapta grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ paśūn evāvarūndhe saptapadā śakvarī paśavaḥ śakvarī paśūn evāvarūndhe atha yat saptadaśabhiḥ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti gāyatrīṃ saṃpadyate tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate

athaiṣo apacitir apacitikāmo yajetāpacityaivāsmā apacitiṃ vindati tasya caturviṃśau pavamānau caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī tejasaivāsmai brahmavarcasenāpacitiṃ vindati ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavata ubhābhyām evāsmai bṛhadrathantarābhyām apacitiṃ vindati bhargayaśasī bhavato bhargeṇaivāsmai bhargo dadhāti yaśasā yaśaḥ ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś cobhayair evāsmai stomair apacitiṃ vindati tad āhur vilomāna stomā īśvarā yajamānaṃ vikṣetor vi hy atiyantīti ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo antata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati

athaiṣa sarvastomo apacitir apacitikāmo yajeta sarvair evāsmai stomair apacitiṃ vindati virājaṃ saṃpadyata eṣa vā apacito yo annādo annaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāsmin dadhāti ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavato bhargayaśasī bhavata ubhaye stomāś chandomāś ca pṛṣṭhyāś cobhayair evāsmai stomair apacitiṃ vindati tasya chandomāḥ pṛṣṭhāni paśavo vai chandomā annaṃ pṛṣṭhāny abhipūrvam evāsminn annādyaṃ paśūn dadhāti yac chandomavāṃs tena dvādaśāhayājinam āpnoti tad āhur nānālokāḥ stomāś chandomāś ca pṛṣṭhyāś ca yad ekasmin yajñakratau samavarudhyanta īśvaro [corr caland; bi kss īśvarā] yajamāno apratiṣṭhātor iti ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhām eva tad abhyāyanti

pakṣī vā eṣa stomaḥ pakṣy eṣa nidhīyate na vā apakṣaḥ pakṣiṇam āpnoty atha yad eṣa pakṣy apakṣiṇi nidhīyate tasmāt pakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaiḥ patanti pakṣī jyotiṣmān puṇyān lokān saṃcarati ya evaṃ veda trivṛtāv abhito bhavatas tejo brahmavarcasaṃ trivṛt teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe atha pañcadaśau vīryaṃ vai pañcadaśo vīryam evāvarundhe atha saptadaśau paśavo vai saptadaśaḥ paśūn evāvarundhe athaikaviṃśau pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo madhyata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati atha triṇavāv ime vai lokās triṇava eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati atha trayastriṃśo varṣma vai trayastriṃśaḥ varṣma svānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda eṣa vāva bradhnasya viṣṭapo yad etau trayastriṃśau madhyataḥ saṃdhīyete tena bradhnasya viṣṭapam ārohati madhyato vā agnir variṣṭhas tasmād ete stomā madhyato variṣṭhāḥ kriyante trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti

athaiṣa jyotiḥ tasya trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni caturviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni prāṇo vai trivṛd ātmā pañcadaśaḥ mukhaṃ gāyatry annaṃ vai saptadaśo mukhata eva tad annaṃ dhatte annam atty annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda mādhyandinena vai pavamānena devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan yad eṣa caturviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāno bhavati svargasya lokasyākrāntyai caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate pakṣi vā etac chandaḥ pakṣī jyotiṣmān puṇyān lokān saṃcarati ya evaṃ veda madhyato vā agnir variṣṭhas tasmād ete stomā madhyato variṣṭhāḥ kriyante ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyata ekākinam evainam annādyasyādhyakṣaṃ karoti jyotir vā eṣo agniṣṭomo jyotiṣmantaṃ puṇyaṃ lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate

athaiṣa ṛṣabhaḥ ṛṣabho vā eṣa stomānām ṛṣabhatāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda rājanyaṃ yājayed ṛṣabho vai paśūnām adhipatī rājanyo manuṣyāṇām yo vā asti so adhipatiḥ adhipatiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda tasya sadoviśīyaṃ mādhyandine pavamāne bhavati viśam evāsmai savanābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati samantaṃ bhavati samantām evāsmai viśaṃ karoty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavata iyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ dyaur bṛhadevāsmāl lokād gāyatry evāmuṣmād ubhayor anayor lokayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati anuṣṭubhi bṛhad bhavaty anto vā anuṣṭup chandasām anto bṛhat sāmnām anto rājanyo manuṣyāṇām anta eva tad antaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmād yo rājanyānāṃ hīyate na sa punaragraṃ paryeti

yo vai vājapeyaḥ sa rājasūyo yo rājasūyaḥ sa varūṇasavo athaiṣa gosavaḥ svārājyo vā eṣa yajñaḥ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda prajāpatir hi svārājyaṃ parameṣṭhī svārājyam parameṣṭhitāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavatas tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda ayutaṃ dakṣiṇās tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda pratiduhābhiṣicyate tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda bṛhataḥ stotra pratyabhiṣicyate tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda anuddhate dakṣiṇata āhavanīyasyābhiṣicyate asyām evānantarhite adhy abhiṣicyate sarvaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśastena gosavaḥ

athaiṣa marutstoma etena vai maruto aparimitāṃ puṣṭim apuṣyann aparimitāṃ puṣṭiṃ puṣyati ya evaṃ veda yad gaṇaśaḥ stomās tena marutstomo gaṇaśo hi marutaḥ etenaiva trīn yājayet yat trīṇi trivṛnti stotrāṇi bhavanti nānā brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhanti yat trīṇi pañcadaśāni nānā vīrye yat trīṇi saptadaśāni nānā paśuṣu yat trīṇy ekaviṃśāni nānā pratitiṣṭhanti pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda

athaiṣa indrāgnyoḥ kulāyaḥ prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā yajeta prajā vai kulāyaṃ paśavaḥ kulāyaṃ gṛhāḥ kulāyaṃ kulāyam eva bhavati etenaiva dvau yājayet yat ṣaṭ trivṛnti stotrāṇi bhavanti nānā brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhato yat dve pañcadaśe nānā vīrye yat dve saptadaśe nānā paśuṣu yat dve ekaviṃśe nānā pratitiṣṭhataḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda

athaiṣa pañcadaśa indrastoma ukthyaḥ etena vā indro aty anyā devatā abhavad aty anyāḥ prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda rājanyaṃ yājayet sarvaḥ pañcadaśo bhavaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśa ojasaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati aindrīṣu bhavantīndriyeṇaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati ukthyo bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni viḍ ukthāni viśam evāsmai paśūn anuniyunakty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati pañcadaśa stotrāṇi pañcadaśāni bhavanty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśo abhipūrvam evāsminn ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti

athaiṣa indrāgnyoḥ stoma etena vā indrāgnī aty anyā devatā abhavatām aty anyāḥ prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda trivṛt pañcadaśo bhavati brahma vai trivṛt kṣatraṃ pañcadaśo brahmaṇa iva cāsya kṣatrasyeva ca prakāśo bhavati ya evaṃ veda rājā ca purohitaś ca yajeyātām gāyatrīṃ ca jagatīṃ ca saṃpadyate tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatryā brāhmaṇo avarundhe viśaṃ rājā jagatyā praviśati purodhākāmo yajeta bṛhaspatir akāmayata devānāṃ purodhāṃ gaccheyam iti sa etenāyajata sa devānāṃ purodhām agacchad gacchati purodhāṃ ya evaṃ veda

athaiṣa vighanaḥ indro akāmayata pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vihanyām iti sa etaṃ vighanam apaśyat tena pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vyahan vi pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda yat trivṛd bhavati prāṇāṃs tenāvarundhe yat dvādaśaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tena yat pañcadaśo vīryaṃ tena yat saptadaśo annādyaṃ tena yad ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhā tena yan navadaśaḥ prajananaṃ tena yac caturviṃśo brahmavarcasaṃ tena yat triṇavo vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati paśukāmo yajeta bṛhatīṃ saṃpadyate paśavo vai bṛhatī paśūn evāvarundhe ṣaḍ etā bṛhatyo bhavanti ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ paśavo anu prajāyante tān evāptvāvarundhe

indram adevyo māyā ayacanta sa prajāpatim upādhāvavat tasmā etaṃ vighanaṃ prāyacchat tena sarvā mṛdho vyahata yad vyahata tad vighanasya vighanatvam sarvā mṛdho vihate ya evaṃ vidvān vighanena yajate yam evaṃ vidvān vighanena yājayati paśukāmo yajeta paśavo vai bṛhatī paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati

trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni pañcadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśa ārbhava ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ sokthyaḥ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ jyotiṣṭomenātirātreṇarddhikāmo yajetābhikramo vā eṣa stomānām abhikrāntyā abhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti eṣo agniṣṭoma eṣa ukthya eṣo atirātro agniṣṭomena vai devā imaṃ lokam abhyajayann ukthyair antarikṣaṃ rātryāmuṃ lokam ajayann ahorātrābhyām abhyavartanta parācyo vā anyā vyucchanti pratīcyo anyā eṣā vāva pratīcī vyucchati yāśvinena vyucchati pratīcīr evāsmā uṣaso vivāsayati dve saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyete eṣā vai stanavatī virāṭ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etāṃ dugdhe trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti

trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ sarvastomenātirātreṇa bubhūṣan yajeta sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati yat trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati tat trivṛtaṃ stomam āpnoti gāyatrīṃ chando yat pañcadaśāny ājyāni tat pañcadaśaṃ stomam āpnoti triṣṭubhaṃ chando yat saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānas tat saptadaśaṃ stomam āpnoti jagatīṃ chando yad ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭāni tad ekaviṃśaṃ stomam āpnoty anuṣṭubhaṃ chando yat triṇava ārbhavas tat triṇavaṃ stomam āpnoti paṅktiṃ chando yat trayastriṃśo agniṣṭomas tat trayastriṃśaṃ stomam āpnoti virājaṃ chando yad uṣṇikkakubhau kriyete tad uṣṇikkakubhāv āpnoti yad āśvinaṃ śasyate tat sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati prāñcaṃ vai trayastriṃśo yajñaṃ prabhujati tam adhvaryur ekādaśinyā purastāt pratyudyacchaty ekādaśa raśanā ekādaśa paśava ekādaśa yūpā bhavanti tat trayastriṃśe trayastriṃśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati tayā samudyatayā rātryā yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ tam abhyaśnute yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ tam abhyaśnute ya evaṃ veda

trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ chandomā itarāṇi triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamam athaikaviṃśam atha saptadaśam ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhis trivṛt prathamam atiriktastotram atha pañcadaśam atha saptadaśam athaikaviṃśam prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te asmāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān agniṣṭomena nāpnot tān ukthair nāpnot tān ṣoḍaśinā nāpnot tān rātryā nāpnot tān sandhinā nāpnot tān āśvinena nāpnot tān agnim abravīd imān ma īpseti tān agnis trivṛtā stomena jarābodhīyena sāmnā nāpnot tān indram abravīd imān ma īpseti tān indraḥ pañcadaśena stomena sattrāsāhīyena sāmnā nāpnot tān viśvān devān abravīd imān ma ipsateti tān viśve devāḥ saptadaśena stomena mārgīṃyaveṇa sāmnā nāpnuvaṃs tān viṣṇum abravīd imān ma īpseti tān viṣṇur ekaviṃśena stomenāpnod vāravantīyenāvārayatedaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti vyakramata yasmāt pra preva paśavo bhraṃśeran sa etena yajeta etena vai devā jaitvāni jitvā yaṃ yaṃ kāmam akāmayanta taṃ tam āpnuvan yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenāpnoti tad aptoryāmno aptoryāmatvam

trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ navasaptadaśāni stotrāṇy ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ sokthaḥ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ navasaptadaśenātirātreṇa prajākāmo yajeta nava vai prāṇāḥ prajāpatiḥ saptadaśaḥ prāṇebhya eva tad adhi prajāpateḥ prajāḥ prajāyante kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhati puruṣo vai kakup garbho vā eṣa madhyato dhīyate tasyāṃ sākamaśvam prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā na prājāyanta sa etat sāmāpaśyat tā aśvo bhūtvābhyajighrat tāḥ prājāyanta prajananaṃ vā etat sāma prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda dvipadāṃ kakubho loke karoti garbham eva taddhitaṃ madhyataḥ prajanayati atirātro bhavaty ahorātre vā anu prajāḥ prajāyante ahorātre evānu prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāyate

trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni pañcadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśa ārbhava ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ saptadaśāny ukthāni pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ viṣuvatātirātreṇa jyeṣṭhaṃ jyaiṣṭhineyaṃ yājayed viṣuvān vā eṣa stomānāṃ viṣuvān eva bhavati yad eka ekaviṃśo bhavaty ekaviṃśo vā ito asāv āditya dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa ādityasyaivainaṃ mātrāṃ gamayati eṣa vā udeti na vā enam anyat jyotiṣāṃ jyotiḥ pratyudeti nainam anyaḥ sveṣu pratyudeti ya evaṃ veda

pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ trivṛnty ājyāni saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir goṣṭomenātirātreṇa bhrātṛvyavān yajeta gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo anudanta rātryānapajayyam ajayann ebhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudya rātryānapajayyaṃ jayati

trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir āyuṣṭomenātirātreṇa svargakāmo yajetordhvāḥ stomā yanty anapabhraṃśāya yad atirātro bhavaty ahorātrābhyām eva svargaṃ lokam eti

trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya pañcadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ saptadaśam acchāvākasyaikaviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭham ekaviṃśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya triṇavaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ekaviṃśam acchāvakasya triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir abhijitātirātreṇa bhrātṛvyavān yajetābhijitā vai devā asurān imān lokān abhyajayat rātryānapajayyam ajayann abhijitaiva bhrātṛvyam imān lokān abhijitya rātryānapajayyaṃ jayati

trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyaikaviṃśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ pañcadaśam acchāvākasya saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ triṇavaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya saptadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ekaviṃśam acchāvākasya triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātriḥ trivṛt sandhir viśvajitātirātreṇa paśukāmo yajeta reto hi nābhānediṣṭhīyaṃ paśavo vālakhilyā yan nābhānediṣṭhīyaṃ pūrvaṃ śasyata uttarā vālakhilyā retasas tat paśavaḥ prajāyante rūpāṇi vikaroti yad vārṣākapam ṛtuṣu pratitiṣṭhati yad evayāmarut

trivṛt ātirātreṇa brahmavarcasakāmo yajeta tejo vai trivṛt brahmavarcasaṃ teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe tejasi brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhati pañcadaśenātirātreṇa vīryakāmo yajetaujo vīryaṃ pañcadaśa oja eva vīryam avarundha ojasi vīrye pratitiṣṭhati saptadaśenātirācreṇānnādyakāmo yajetānnaṃ vai saptadaśo annādyam evāvarundha ekaviṃśenātirātreṇa pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeta pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo yad atirātro bhavaty ahorātrayor eva pratitiṣṭhati

jyotiṣṭomo agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahaḥ sarvastomo atirātra uttaram tasya caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamam athaikaviṃśam atha saptadaśam ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ haviṣmāṃś ca haviṣkṛc cāṅgirasāv ahīyetā tāv āgacchetāṃ yato aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tāv atapyetāṃ tāv ete sāmanī apaśyatāṃ tābhyāṃ dvirātram atanvātāṃ tena svargaṃ lokam aitām yaḥ pauṇyo hīna iva syāt sa etena yajetāpnoti pūrveṣāṃ prahām āpnutāṃ hi tāv aṅgirasaḥ prajākāmo yajeta dvitīyaṃ hy etad yat prajāḥ svargakāmo yajeta dvitīyād dhi lokāt paro loko abhiprakramyo durādho dvirātra ity āhur yad agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty ukthyam antaryanti yady ukthyo agniṣṭomam yaj jyotir ukthyaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavati nāgniṣṭomam antaryanti nokthāni tad āhur eṣā vāva yajñasya mātrā yad agniṣṭomo yad agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavati yajñasya mātrāṃ nātikrāmaty athottarasyāhna ukthebhyo adhi rātrim upayanti tenokthāny anantaritāni caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavaty uttarasyāhnaś caturviṃśaty akṣarā gāyatrī prajananaṃ gāyatrī prajātyai ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate sarvastomo atirātro bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati

atha yasya jyotir ukthyaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty āyur atirātra uttaram tisraḥ pūrvasyāhno virājam atiricyante dvābhyām uttaram ahar virāja ūnam ūnātiriktaṃ vā anuprajāḥ prajāyante pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya evaṃ veda ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyate ekākinam evainam annādyasyādhyakṣaṃ karoti etena vai citrarathaṃ kāpeyā ayājayaṃs tam ekākinam annādyasyādhyakṣam akurvaṃs tasmāc caitrarathīnām ekaḥ kṣatrapatir jāyate anulamba iva dvitīyaḥ

atha yasya trivṛt pañcadaśo agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty āyur atirātra uttaram mithunābhyāṃ stomābhyām uttaram ahaḥ prajanayanti tat prajātaṃ śva ārabhante cakre vā ete sākaṃvṛtī yat trivṛt pañcadaśau stomau yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenābhyaśnute yatra yatra hi cakrīvatā kāmayate tat tad abhyaśnute atha yad āyur atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhityai etena vai kapivano bhauvāyana iṣṭvārūkṣatām agacchat arūkṣo bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate

trivṛt prātaḥsavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ soktham ekaviṃśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ triṇavaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ trayastriṃśa ārbhavaś catustriṃśo agniṣṭoma ekaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni ṣoḍaśaṃ prathamaṃ rātriṣāma pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ prajāpatir vā idam eka āsīt tasya vāg eva svam āsīd vāg dvitīyā sa aikṣatemām eva vācaṃ visṛjā iyaṃ vā idaṃ sarvaṃ vibhavanty eṣyatīti sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sedaṃ sarvaṃ vibhavanty ait sordhvodātanod yathāpāṃ dhārā santataivaṃ tasyā eti tṛtīyam acchinat tad bhūmir abhavad abhūd iva vā idam iti tad bhūmer bhūmitvaṃ keti tṛtīyam acchinat tad antarikṣam abhavad antar eva vā idam iti tad antarikṣasyāntarikṣatvaṃ ho iti tṛtīyam ūrdhvam udāsyat tat dyaur abhavad adyutad iva vā iti tad divo divatvam eṣā vāva pratyakṣaṃ vāg yaj jihvāgreṇaitad vāco vadati yad eti madhyenaitad vāco vadati yat keti sarvayaitad vāco raso adhyūrdhva udvad ati yaddho iti yad etāni rūpāṇy anvahaṃ vyajyante mukhata eva tad vācaṃ visṛjante mukhato yajñiyaṃ karma prajāpatir vā idam ekākṣarāṃ vācaṃ satīṃ tredhā vyakarot ta ime lokā abhavan rūkṣā anupajīvanāḥ sa aikṣata katham ime lokā loma gṛhṇīyuḥ katham upajīvanīyāḥ syur iti sa etaṃ trirātram apaśyat tam āharat tenemān lokān anvātanot tato vā ime lokā lomāgṛhṇaṃs tata upajīvanīyā abhavaṃs trirātrasya vā idaṃ puṣṭaṃ trirātrasyodaraṇaṃ yad idam eṣu lokeṣv adhi gacchati paśūnāṃ bhūmānaṃ dvipadāṃ catuṣpadāṃ ya evaṃ veda prajāpatir yad vācaṃ vyasṛjata sākṣarad eveti prathamaṃ kṣeti dvitīyaṃ reti tṛtīyaṃ yena yena vai rūpeṇa prajāpatir vācaṃ vyasṛjata tena tena rūpeṇājyāni cārabhyante ahāni cāpyante tad āhur brahmavādino akṣarestho vai trirātra ity ekākṣarā vai vāk tryakṣaram akṣaraṃ tryakṣaraḥ puruṣaḥ sa vā enaṃ vedety āhur ya enaṃ puruṣasammitaṃ vedeti

etena vai devā eṣu lokeṣv ārdhnuvann etena svargaṃ lokamāyan vāg vai trirātro vāco rūpeṇājyāni cāhāni ca vibhajyanta ekākṣarā vai vāk tryakṣaram akṣaram akṣarasya rūpeṇa vibhajyante trayo gandharvās teṣām eṣā bhaktir agneḥ pṛthivī vāyor antarikṣam asāv ādityasya dyaus trayo gharmāsa uṣasaṃ sacante agnir uṣasaṃ sacate vāyur uṣasaṃ sacate asāv āditya uṣasaṃ sacate trīṇi mithunāni tāny eṣaḥ mithunaṃ dve sambhavato mithunād yat prajāyate tat tṛtīyam indro vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat so abravīn mā me praharṣīr asti vā idaṃ mayi vīryaṃ tat te pradāsyāmīti tad asmai prāyacchat tad viṣṇuḥ pratyagṛhṇāt sa dvitīyaṃ sa tṛtīyam udayacchat sa evābravīn mā me prahārṣīr asti vā idaṃ mayi vīryaṃ tat te pradāsyāmīti tad asmai prāyacchat tad viṣṇuḥ pratyagṛhṇād etad vāca tad abhyanūcyate ubhau jigyathur na parājayethe na parājigye kataraś ca nainoḥ indraś ca viṣṇo yad apaspṛdhethāṃ tredhā sahasraṃ vitad airayethām iti etad vā ābhyāṃ tat sahasraṃ prāyacchat tasyaiṣā bhaktir ya ārṣeyo vidvāṃs tasmai prathame ahani deyaṃ yathā vā iyaṃ evaṃ sa pratiṣṭhiteyaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ saḥ yo anārṣeyo vidvāṃs tasmai dvitīye ahani deyaṃ yathā vā antarikṣam evaṃ so antarikṣam ity antarikṣaṃ vidur vedaṃ tasya viduḥ ya ārṣeyo vidvāṃs tasmai tṛtīye ahani deyaṃ yathā vai dyaur evaṃ sa dyaur iti divaṃ vidur bandhu tasya viduḥ śatāny anvahaṃ dīyante eṣā vāva yajñasya mātrā yac chataṃ saiva sāvicchinnā dīyate daśato anvahaṃ dīyante daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājo yajñaḥ saiva sā vicchinnā dīyate trayastriṃśac ca trīṇi ca śatāni prathame ahani deyās tathā dvitīye tathā tṛtīye athaiṣā dvidevatyā trirūpā brahmaṇo dve tṛtīye tṛtīyam agnīdhaḥ kāmyāsi priyāsi havyāsīḍe rante sarasvati mahi viśruta etāni te aghnye nāmāni deveṣu naḥ sukṛto brūtāt

idaṃ vāva prathamenāhnā vyakarod yad idam asyām adhyāyat ta mūlam idaṃ dvitīyena yad idaṃ prāṇād ejaty adas tṛtīyena yad varṣati yan nakṣatrāṇi yad amuṃ lokaṃ bheje tad āhur brahmavādino mahāvrataṃ vā etad yad eṣa trirātra iti tasyai tad eva mukhaṃ yad eteṣām ahvāṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ ye abhito ahanī tau pakṣau yan madhyamam ahaḥ sa ātmāgniṣṭomasāmāni puccham yad evāsāv udeti tan mukhaṃ ye abhito ahanī tau pakṣau yan madhyamam ahaḥ sa ātmāgniḥ puccham yad evāsāv udeti tan mukhaṃ ye abhito ahanī tau pakṣau yan madhyamam ahaḥ sa ātmā yad astam eti tat puccham etāvān vāva trirātro gāyatraḥ prāṇas traiṣṭubhaṃ cakṣur jāgataṃ śrotraṃ sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ veda tad āhur brahmavādinaḥ kiyāṃs trirātra itīyān iti brūyād iyaddhayetad abhy atho iyān iti brūyād iyaddhayevaitad abhiparāṅ arvāṅ ity āhuḥ parāṅ iti brūyāt parāṅ hi vadati parāṅ paśyati parāṅ prāṇity ekā dvā u trayā ity āhur eka iti brūyāt samāno hy eṣa yat prāṇo apāno vyānas tad yathā vā ado maṇau sūtram otam evam eṣu lokeṣu trirātra otaḥ śobhate asya mukhaṃ ya evaṃ veda yad vai trirātrasya saloma tad asya viloma yad asya viloma tad asya saloma tad yad etat paraṃ sad ahar avaraṃ kriyate yajamānāyaiva tat paśūn parigṛhṇāti prajananāya na hy amuṣmin loke paśavaḥ prajāyante ete vāva chandasāṃ vīryavattame yad gāyatrī ca triṣṭup ca yad ete abhito bhavato madhye jagatī vīryavatībhyām eva tac chandobhyāṃ paśūn parigṛhṇāti prajananāya na hy amuṣmin loke paśavaḥ prajāyante asau vāva trirātro yathodety evaṃ prathamam ahar yathā madhyandina evaṃ dvitīyaṃ yathāstam ety evaṃ tṛtīyaṃ gacchaty amuṣyasāyujyaṃ gacchati sāveśyaṃ ya evaṃ veda

indro marutaḥ sahasram ajināt svāṃ viśaṃ somāya rājñe procya tasmād rājñe procya viṃśa jinanti tau yamo aśṛṇon maruto ha sahasram ajyāśiṣṭām iti sa āgacchat so abravīd upa māsmin sahasre hvayethām iti tam upāhvayetāṃ sa yamo apaśyad ekāṅgāṃ sahasre api sahasrasya payo bibhratīṃ so abravīd iyam eva mamāstu sahasraṃ yuvāṃ vikalpayethām iti tāv abrūtāṃ yathā vāva tvam etāṃ paśyasy evam āvam etāṃ paśyāva iti tayā vā idaṃ sahasraṃ vikalpayāmahā ity abruvaṃs tām udake prāveśayaṃs te abravan na śānāharāmahai yasmai na iyaṃ prathamāyādeṣyati iti te aṃśān āharanta somasya prathama aid athendrasyātha yamasya te abruvan somāya rājña udehi tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasa iti sā babhruḥ piṅgākṣy ekavarṣodait tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasaḥ sā yā somakrayaṇī saiva sā tṛtīyena cāsya tasyā ātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasaḥ somaḥ krīto bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān somaṃ krīṇāti yasmā evaṃ viduṣe somaṃ krīṇanti te abruvann indrāyodehi tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasa iti sā śabalī paṣṭhauhy udait tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasaḥ sāyendriyaiṣyā saiva sā tṛtīyena cāsya tasyā ātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasa indriyaiṣyā dattā bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān indriyaiṣyāṃ dadāti yasmā evaṃ viduṣa indriyaiṣyāṃ dadāti te abruvan yamāyodehi tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasa iti sā jaratī kuṣṭhāśṛṅgyad aid dhūmrā vā dityauhīrmato hrasīyasī tṛtīyena cātmanaḥ tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payasaḥ sā yānustaraṇī saiva sā tṛtīyena cāsya tasyā ātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya payaso anustaraṇī kṛtā bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān anustaraṇīṃ karoti yasmā evaṃ viduṣe anustaraṇīṃ kurvanti nācakṛvān manyate tad āhur brahmavādino na vā amuṣmin loke sahasrayāḍ aloko astīti tad yāvad itaḥ sahasrasya gaur gavi pratiṣṭhitā tāvad asmāl lokād asau lokaḥ sarasrayājī vā imān lokān vyāpnoty atho yāvat sahasraṃ yojanāny atho sahasram āśvīnān yatho yāvat sahasram ahnayāni tad gavā gavā spṛṇoti samākramaṇāya vā etā dīyante sahasraṃ yad asṛjata tasya tārpyaṃ yonir āsīd yat tārpyaṃ pratyasya nayati sayonitvāya

prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmāt sṛṣṭāḥ parācya āyan natsyati na iti bibhyatyaḥ so abravīd upa mā vartadhvaṃ tathā vai vo atsyāmi yathādyamānā bhūyasyaḥ prajaniṣyatha iti tābhyo vainaṃ ṛtaṃ brūhīty abruvaṃs tābhya ṛtanidhanenartam abravīd īnidhanenāvayat triṇidhanena prājanayad etair ha vā idaṃ sāmabhir mṛtyuḥ prajā atti ca prajanayati adyamānasya bhūyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda jyeṣṭhasāmāni vā etāni śreṣṭhasāmāni prajāpatisāmāni gacchati jyaiṣṭhayaṃ śraiṣṭhayaṃ ya evaṃ veda etair vai sāmabhiḥ prajāpatir imān lokān sarvān kāmān dugdhe yad ācyā dugdhe tad ācyā dohānām ācyā dohatvam sarvān imān lokān kāmān dugdhe ya evaṃ vidvān etais sāmabhiḥ stute ime vai lokā etāni sāmāny ayam evartanidhanam antarikṣam īnidhanaṃ dyaus triṇidhanam yathā kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrāṇy anusañcaraty evam imān lokān anusañcarati ya evaṃ veda agner vā etāni vaiśvānarasya sāmāni yatra vā etair aśāntaiḥ stuvanti tat prajā devo ghātuko bhavaty agnim upanidhāya stuvate svāyā eva tad devatāyāḥ sāmyekṣāya namaskṛtyodgāyati śāntais stuvanti

vāg vai śabalī tasyās trirātro vatsas trirātro vā etāṃ pradāpayati tad ya evaṃ veda tasmā eṣā prattā dugdhe yo alam annādyāya sann athānnaṃ nādyāt barāsīṃ paridhāya taptaṃ piban dvādaśa rātrīr adhaḥ śayīta yā dvādaśī syāt tasyā upavyuṣaṃ śabalīhomaṃ hutvā purā vāgbhyaḥ sampravaditor yatra grāmyasya paśor nāśṛṇuyāt tad araṇyaṃ paretya darbhastambam ālabhya śabali śabalīti trir āhvayed yad anyac chunaś ca gardabhāc ca prativāśyate sā samṛddhā yadi na prativāśyeta saṃvatsare punar āhvayeta śabali samudro asi viśvavyacā brahma devānāṃ prathamajā ṛtasyānnam asi śukram asi tejo asy amṛtam asi tāṃ tvā vidma śabali dīdyānāṃ tasyāste pṛthivī pādo antarikṣaṃ pādo dyauḥ pādaḥ samudraḥ pāda eṣāsi śabali tāṃ tvā vidma sā na iṣam ūrjaṃ dhukṣva vasordhārāṃ śabali prajānāṃ śaciṣṭhā vratam anugeṣaṃ svāhā

catuṣṭomo agniṣṭoma ekaviṃśa ukthyaḥ sarvastomo atirātraḥ prajāpater vā akṣy aśvat tat parāpatat tad aśvo abhavat tad aśvasyāśvatvaṃ tad devā aśvamedhena pratyadadhur eṣa vāva prajāpatiṃ sarvaṃ karoti yo aśvamedhena yajate eṣa vāva saśarīraḥ sambhavaty amuṣmai lokāyayo aśvamedhī saraghā vā aśvasya sakthy āvṛhat tad devāś catuṣṭomena pratyadadhur yac catuṣṭomo bhavaty aśvasya sarvatvāya yat tisro anuṣṭubhaś catasro gāyatrīḥ karoti tasmāt tribhis tiṣṭhan pratitiṣṭhati sarvān palāyamānaḥ pratidadhāti anto vā aśvaḥ paśūnām anto anuṣṭup chandasām anto viṣṇur devatānām antaś catuṣṭomas stomānām antas trirātro yajñānāṃ yad vaiplavyo anuṣṭubhaḥ pratipado bhavanti catuṣṭoma stomas trirātro yajño anta eva tadantaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati ekaviṃśam ahar bhavati yasminn aśva ālabhyata ekaviṃśo vā ito asāv ādityo dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa ādityasyaivainaṃ mātrāṃ gamayati tasya mahānāmnyaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavanti anyad-anyad vā etāś chando anyonya ete paśava ālabhyanta etā vā etaṃ samāpnuvanti yan mahānāmnyaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavanty aśvasya sarvatvāya pārthuraśmaṃ brahmasāma bhavati īśvaro vā eṣo ayato adhṛtaḥ parāṃ parāvatam eto raśminā vā aśvo dhṛto yat pārthuraśmaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty aśvasyaiva yatyai sarvastomo atirātro bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati ekayūpo vaikādaśinī vānyeṣāṃ yajñānāṃ bhavaty ekaviṃśiny aśvamedhasya khādiro vā bailvo vā pārṇo vā anyeṣāṃ yajñānāṃ bhavati naicudāra ekaviṃśatyaratnir aśvamedhasya nānyeṣāṃ paśūnāṃ tejanyā avadyanty avadyanty aśvamedhasya dakṣiṇato anyeṣāṃ paśūnām avadyanty uttarato aśvamedhasya plakṣaśākhāsv anyeṣāṃ paśūnām avadyanti vetasaśākhāsv aśvamedhasya yūpe grāmyān paśūn niyuñjanty ārokeṣv āraṇyān dhārayanty ā grāmyān paśūn labhante prāraṇyān sṛjanti

trayas trivṛto atirātrāḥ sarve ṣoḍaśimantaḥ yo rājya āśaṃseta sa etena yajeta rājā vā eṣa stomānāṃ rājyam evāsmin dadhāti yadākṣārāṇi prathamam ahar bhajanta ekākṣarā vai vāg vāco anativādāya atha yat dvyakṣaraṇidhanam ājyadohaṃ bhavaty uttarayor ahor abhisantatyā anvaham ājyadohāni bhavanty anvaham evainaṃ paśubhiḥ samardhayanti sarve ṣoḍaśimanto bhavantīndriyaṃ vīryaṃ ṣoḍaśīndriyeṇaivainān vīryeṇa samardhayati

caturviṃśāḥ pavamānās trivṛnty ājyāni pañcadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśo agniṣṭomaś catuścatvāriṃśāḥ pavamānāḥ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāny ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ soktho aṣṭācatvāriṃśāḥ pavamānā ekaviṃśāny ājyāni triṇavāni pṛṣṭhāni trayastriṃśo agniṣṭoma ekaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiś chandomapavamānaḥ paśukāmo yajet paśavo vai chandomā yac chandomāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśūnevāvarūndhe ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tat mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate

trivṛt prātassavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ caturviṃśaṃ prātassavanaṃ catuścatvāriṃśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ soktham ekaviṃśaṃ prātassavanan triṇavaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ trayastriṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ soktham ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir antarvasuḥ ime lokās trirātraḥ astīva vā ayaṃ loko astīvāsau chidram ivāntarikṣam astīva trirātrasya prathamam ahar astīvottamaṃ chidram iva madhyataḥ paśavo vai chandomā yac chandomā madhyato bhavanty apihityā evācchidratāyai

trivṛt prātassavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ ekaviṃśaṃ prātassavanaṃ triṇavaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ trayastriṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ caturviṃśaṃ prātassavanaṃ catuścatvāriṃśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ soktham ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ parākaḥ parākeṇa vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokamāyan svargakāmo yajeta parāṅ evaitena svargaṃ lokam ākramate yad vā etasyākaṃ tad asya parāk tat parākasya parākatvam na vai tatra jagmuṣe kiñcanā'kam nāsmā akaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda prajāyās tv akḷptaḥ parāṅ hy evaitena svargaṃ lokam ākramate tad yad ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī bhavati pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhis tenāsmin loke pratitiṣṭhati caturviṃśāḥ pavamānās trivṛnty ājyāni pañcadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśo agniṣṭomaś caturviṃśāḥ pavamānāḥ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāny ekaviṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ sokthaś caturviṃśāḥ pavamānāḥ saptadaśāny ājyāny ekaviṃśani pṛṣṭhāni triṇavo agniṣṭomaḥ sokthaś caturviṃśāḥ pavamānā ekaviṃśāny ājyāni triṇavāni pṛṣṭhāni trayastriṃśo agniṣṭoma ekaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhi atrir akāmayata catvāro me vīrā ājāyerann iti sa etam apaśyat tasya catvāro vīrā ājāyantāsya catvāro vīrā jāyante ya evaṃ veda ekaṃ stomam utsṛjyaikam abhyārabhate vīrajananaṃ vai stomo vīram evāsmai tat prajanayati caturviṃśāḥ pavamānā bhavanti caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī prajananaṃ gāyatrī prajātyai ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate agniṣṭomaḥ prathamam ahar ūktho dvitīyaṃ ṣoḍaśī tṛtīyam atirātraś caturthaṃ nānāvīryatāyai nānāvīryāṇy ahāni karoti gāyatraṃ vai prathamam ahas traiṣṭubhaṃ dvitīyaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyam ānuṣṭubhaṃ caturtham tad āhur yat tṛtīye ahani ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇīyus tṛtīyenāhnānuṣṭubham āpnuyur acchandaś caturtham ahaḥ syād ānuṣṭubho vai ṣoḍaśīti caturthe ahani ṣoḍaśī grahītavyaḥ sva āyatane ṣoḍaśī gṛhyate chandobhir ahāni nānāvīryāṇi karoti naudhasaṃ prathamasyāhno brahmasāma śyaitaṃ dvitīyasya śrāyantīyaṃ tṛtīyasya traiśokaṃ caturthasya tad āhur apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yat jyāyasaḥ chandaso adhi kanīyaś chanda upaitīti tadyadeṣā caturthe'hanyatijagatī kriyate'napabhraṃśāya kāleyaṃ prathamasyāho acchāvākasāma mādhucchandasaṃ dvitīyasya rauravaṃ tṛtīyasya samantaṃ caturthasya nānāvīryatāyai nānāvīryāṇy ahāni karoti "abhitvā vṛṣabhā suta" iti tṛtīyasyāhno rathantaraṃ "kastam indra tvā vasava" iti vāmadevyaṃ "yajñā yathā apūrva" iti caturthasyāhno bṛhat "ed u madhor madintaram" iti vāmadevyaṃ chandasāṃ nānāvīryatāyai nānāvīryāṇy ahāni kāroti

trivṛt pañcadaśo agniṣṭomaḥ prathamam ahaḥ athottarasyāhnoś caturviṃśaṃ vahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāni trīṇy ājyāni saptadaśam acchāvākasyaikaviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśe dve pṛṣṭhe ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃṃ soktham tṛtīyasyāhna ekaviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ trīṇi cājyāni pañcadaśam acchāvākasya caturviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇavaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ dve cokthe ekaviṃśam acchāvākasya caturthasyāhnaś caturviśāḥ pavamānāḥ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśāni trīṇy ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni trayastriṃśo agniṣṭoma ekaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ jamadagniḥ puṣṭikāma etam āharat sa imān poṣān apuṣyat yad idam āhur navā ūrvau palitau sañjānāte iti tat sarvān evaitena poṣān puṣyati jagatī chandobhiḥ sampadyate jagatī vai chandasāṃ paramaṃ poṣaṃ puṣṭā paramam evaite poṣaṃ puṣyati puroḍāśinya upasado bhavanti paśavo vai puroḍāśāḥ paśuṣveva pratitiṣṭhanti agne ver hotra ver adhvaram āpitaraṃ vaiśvānaram avase akar indrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā devāv aśvinau madhukaśayādyemaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānāya mimikṣatam indrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā deva viṣṇa urv adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāyādhi vikramasvendrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā deva soma retodhā adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāyaidhīndrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā deva savitaḥ susāvitram adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāsuvasvendrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā deva dhātaḥ sudhātādyāsmin yajñe yajamānāyaidhīndrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā devā grāvāṇo madhumatīm adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāya vācaṃ vadatendrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā devy anumate anvadyemaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānāya manyasvendrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā devy adite svādityām adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāyāsuvasvendrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā devya āpo nannamyadhvam adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāyendrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā sadassadaḥ prajāvān ṛbhur juṣāṇa indrāya devebhyo juhutā havis svāhā deva tvaṣṭaḥ suretodhā adyāsmin yajñe yajamānāyaidhīndrāya devebhyo juhutā haviḥ svāhā āgneya ekakapāla āśvino dvikapālo vaiṣṇavas trikapālaḥ saumyaś catuṣkapālaḥ sāvitraḥ pañcakapālo dhātraḥ ṣaṭkapālo mārūtaḥ saptakapālo bārhaspatyo aṣṭākapālo maitro navakapālo vārūṇo daśakapāla aindra ekādaśakapālo vaiśvadevo dvādaśakapālaḥ

trivṛta prātassavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ prātassavanaṃ saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ saptadaśaṃ prātassavanam ekaviṃśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ triṇavaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ soktham ekaviṃśaṃ prātassavanaṃ triṇavaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ trayastriṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ putrahato hīna ivāmanyata sa etam apaśyat so agraṃ paryaid yo hīna iva manyeta sa etena yajeta yat stomāt stomam abhisaṃkrāmaty agrād evāgraṃ rohati vasiṣṭhasya janitre bhavataḥ prajātyai pratyavarohīṇy uttamasyāhna ukthāni bhavanti pratiṣṭhityai

trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthaḥ saptadaśa uktha ekaviṃśo atirātro viśvāmitrasya sañjayaḥ jahnuvṛcīvanto rāṣṭra āhiṃsanta sa viśvāmitro jāhnavo rājaitam apaśyat sa rāṣṭram abhavad arāṣṭram itare bhrātṛvyavān yajeta bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda jyotir vā eṣa vihṛtaḥ jyotiḥ prajānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda catuṣṭomo vā eṣa catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati ekaviṃśaṃ stomā nātiyanti pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo antata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati

dve trivṛtī savane pañcadaśam ekaṃ dve pañcadaśe savane saptadaśam ekaṃ dve saptadaśe savane ekaviṃśam ekaṃ dve ekaviṃśe savane triṇavam ekaṃ dve triṇave savane trayastriṃśam ekaṃ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta te na vyajayanta te abruvan vāco mithunena vijayāmahai yatare no vāco mithunaṃ na prativindāṃs te parā bhavān iti te devā eka ity abruvann ekety asurā vāco mithunaṃ pratyavindan dvāv iti devā abruvan dve ity asurā vāco mithunaṃ pratyavindanaṃs traya iti devā abruvaṃs tisra ity asurā vāco mithunaṃ pratyavindaṃś catvāra iti devā abruvaṃś catastra ity asurā vāco mithunaṃ pratyavindan pañceti devā abruvan nāsurā avindaṃs tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda saṃvatsaraṃ vā eṣāṃ tad vīryam annādyam avṛñjata saṃvatsaraṃ vīryam annādyaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda pañcarātro vā eṣa pāṅktaḥ purūṣaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavas tena purūṣaṃ ca paśūṃś cāpnoti āstharir vā eṣa santato yajño dvau dvau hi stomāv ahar vahato yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenābhyaśnute yatra yatra hy asthūriṇā kāmayate tat tad abhyaśnute abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho bhavati santatyai pratyavarohīṇy uttamasyāhna ukthāni bhavanti pratiṣṭhityai

trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthaḥ saptadaśa ukthaḥ pañcadaśa ukthaḥ saptadaśo atirātraḥ pañcaśāradīyo marutāṃ stomaḥ yaḥ kāmayeta bahu syām iti sa etena yajeta marūto vai devānāṃ bhūyiṣṭhā bahur eva bhavati saptadaśaṃ stomā nātiyanti prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti agastyo vai marūdbhya ukṣṇaḥ praukṣat tān indrāyābadhnāt te vajram ādāyābhyapatan sa etat kayāśubhīyam apaśyat tenāśamayat yat kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyate śāntyā eva saptadaśa pṛśnīn ukṣṇaḥ pañcavarṣān saptadaśa pṛśnīs trivatsā apravītās tān paryagnikṛtān prokṣitānetarā labhante pretarān sṛjanti tataḥ saṃvatsare navanītapṛśnīr arūṇā ānayanti tāṃś caivokṣṇas tān paryagnikṛtān prokṣitān etarā labhante pretarān sṛjanti tataḥ saṃvatsare rājīvā ānayanti tāṃś caivokṣṇas tān paryagnikṛtān prokṣitān etarā labhante pretarān sṛjanti tataḥ saṃvatsare piśaṅgīr ānayanti tāṃś caivokṣṇas tān paryagnikṛtān prokṣitān etarā labhante pretarān sṛjanti tataḥ saṃvatsare sāraṅgīr ānayanti tāṃś caivokṣṇas tān paryagnikṛtān pokṣitān etarā labhante pretarān sṛjanti tataḥ saṃvatsare somā bhavanti trīṃs trīn anvaham ālabhante pañcottame ahani ajo agnīṣomīyaḥ aindrā mārūto ukṣāṇo mārūtyo vatsataryaḥ yadi rūdro abhimanyotāgnaye rūdravate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yadi saṃśīryaita bhaumam ekakapālaṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yady avasīder nairṛtaṃ caruṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yady apsu mriyetāponaptrīyaṃ caruṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yady andhasyāt sauryaṃ caruṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yadi ślavaṇo vā kuṭo vā syād bārhaspatyaṃ caruṃ nipyāthānyam ālabheta yadi palāyeta vāyavyaṃ caruṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yadi prāsahājayeyur indrāya prasahvana ekādaśakapālaṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta yady anyena mṛtyunā mriyeta prājāpatyaṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ nirūpyāthānyam ālabheta etena vā ekayāvā gāndamo vetasvatīṣṭvā sarvām ṛddhim ārdhnot sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnoti ya evaṃ veda

jyotiṣṭomo agniṣṭomo gaur ukthyo mahāvrataṃ gaur ukthya āyur atirātraḥ saṃvatsaro vai vrataṃ tasya vasanta ṛtur mukhaṃ grīṣmaś ca varṣāś ca pakṣau śaran madhyaṃ hemantaḥ puccham tasmāc charadam oṣadhayo abhisampacyante śarad dhi madhyaṃ saṃvatsarasya akṛtaṃ vā ete kurvanti ye purā saṃvatsarāt vratam upayanti etad vai vratam āptaṃ yat pañcarātre pañca hy ṛtavaḥ āptena vratena stute sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ veda

pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ ṛtavo na pratyatiṣṭhaṃs ta etena pratyatiṣṭhan pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeta praty eva tiṣṭhati ṣaḍ vā ṛtava ṛtuṣv evaitena pratitiṣṭhati pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho bhavati pratyakṣam ṛdhyai pratyakṣaṃ hy etenartava ārdhnuvann ṛdhyā eva

trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśa ukthyo jyotir gaur āyur atirātraḥ yaḥ kāmayeta sarvam āyur iyām iti sa etena yajeta yat tryahaḥ purastād bhavati trayaḥ prāṇāpānavyānās ta eva tat saṃdhīyante atha yat jyotir gaur āyur atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhityai

abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho viśvajid atirātraḥ anyasmai vai kāmāya sattram anyasmai yajño na tatsatreṇāpnoti yasmaikaṃ yajño na tad yajñenāpnoti yasmaikaṃ sattram sattram iva vā etad yad anulomaṃ pṛṣṭhāni yad ekadhā pṛṣṭhāni bhavanty ekadhaivāsmiṃs tad ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti annaṃ pṛṣṭhāny annādyam evāsmin dadhāti paśavaḥ pṛṣṭhāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho bhavati santatyai viśvajid atirātro bhavati viśvasyābhijityai

pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho mahāvratam atirātraḥ sapta ṛṣaya etenārdhnuvaṃs tenarddhis tasmād etena yajanta ṛddhyā eva sapta śirasi prāṇāḥ prāṇā indriyāṇīndriyāṇy evaitenāpnoti sapta grāmyāḥ paśavas tān etenāpnoti vrataṃ saptamasyāhnaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati tad dhy anāptam annaṃ vai vratam annādyam evaitenāpnoti pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho bhavati pratyakṣam ṛdhyai pratyakṣaṃ hy etena sapta ṛṣaya ārdhnuvann ṛdhyā eva

pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ saptadaśaṃ mahāvratam atirātraḥ tasya trivṛc chiraḥ pañcadaśau pakṣau saptadaśa ātmaikaviṃśaṃ puccham etena vai prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya evaṃ veda saptadaśo vai prajāpatir yat saptadaśaṃ vrataṃ bhavati prajāpatim evāpnoti yat trivṛc chiro bhavati nava prāṇāḥ prāṇeṣv eva prati tiṣṭhati yat pañcadaśau pakṣau savīvadhatvāya saptadaśa ātmā bhavati prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajā patim evāpnoti ekaviṃśaṃ puccha bhavati pratiṣṭhityai

pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahaś chandomapavamānaṃ mahāvratam atirātraḥ paśukāmo yajeta paśavo vai chandāmāḥ yac chadomāḥ pavamānā mahāvratasya bhavanti paśūnevāvarūndhe ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate

abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho atha trayastriṃśām ahas tasya catustriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ saptadaśaṃ mahāvratam atirātras tasya caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ trivṛc chiraḥ pañcadaśau pakṣau saptadaśa ātmaikaviṃśaṃ puccham etena vai jamadagniḥ sarvān poṣān apuṣyat sarvān evaitena poṣān puṣyati yad abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāhaḥ purastād bhavati santatyā eva athaitat trayastriṃśam ahas trayastriṃśad devatā devatā evāpnoti tasya catustriṃśo agniṣṭomaḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evāpnoti caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati mahāvratasya caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī prajananaṃ gāyatrī prajātyai ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate yat trivṛc chiro bhavati nava prāṇāḥ prāṇeṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati yat pañcadaśau pakṣau savīvadhatvāya saptadaśa ātmā bhavati prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evāpnoty ekaviṃśaṃ pucchaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhityai

jyotiṣṭomo agniṣṭomo gaur ukthya āyur ukthyo abhijid agniṣṭomo viśvajid agniṣṭomaḥ sarvajid agniṣṭomaḥ sarvastomo atirātraḥ etena vā indro aty ānyā devatā abhavad aty anyā prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda yat jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ purastād bhavati prajñātān stomānupaitīmān eva lokān eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati athābhijid abhijitā vai devā imān lokān abhyajayan viśvajitā viśvam ajayan sarvajitā sarvam ajayan sarvastomātirātro bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati

catvāri trivṛnty ahāny agniṣṭomamukhāni viśvajin mahāvrataṃ jyotiṣṭomo atirātraḥ etena vai prajāpatiḥ purūṣam asṛjata sa sarvasyānnādyasyādhipatyam agacchat sarvasyānnādyasyādhipatyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda śiro vā agre sambhavataḥ sambhavati caturdhā vihitaṃ vai śiraḥ prāṇaś cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ vāgātmā vai pṛṣṭhāni yat pṛṣṭhāny upaiti śira evātmānam anusandadhāti etad vai purūṣam akas tasmā annam eva vratam apidadhāti atha yat jyotiṣṭomo atirātro bhavaty akḷptasya kḷptyai

pṛṣṭhayaḥ stomaḥ ṣaḍaho viśvajid atirātraḥ anyasmai vai kāmāya sattram anyasmai yajño na tat sattreṇāpnoti yasmaikaṃ yajño na tad yajñenāpnoti yasmaikaṃ sattraṃ sattram iva vā etad yad anulomaṃ pṛṣṭhāni yadaikadhā pṛṣṭhāni bhavaty ekadhaivāsmiṃs tejo vīryaṃ dadhāty annaṃ pṛṣṭhāny annādyam evāsmin dadhāti paśavaḥ pṛṣṭhāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati yad vai manuṣyāṇāṃ pratyakṣaṃ taddevānāṃ parokṣamatha yanma manuṣyāṇāṃ parokṣaṃ taddevānāṃ pratyakṣam etad vai parokṣaṃ vrataṃ yad viśvajit pratyakṣam evaitenānnādyam avarundhe

pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho mahāvrataṃ jyotiṣṭomo atirātraḥ etena vai devā devatvam agacchan devatvaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda etad vai vratam āptaṃ yad aṣṭarātre agniṣṭomo hi vrataṃ sampadyate atha yat jyotiṣṭhomo atirātro bhavaty akḷptasya kḷptyai aṣṭarātreṇa vai devāḥ sarvam āśnuvata sarvam aśnute ya evaṃ veda

pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho jyotir gaur āyur atirātro devā vai mṛtyor abibhayus te prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs tebhya etena navarātreṇāmṛtatvaṃ prāyacchat etad vāva manuṣyasyāmṛtatvaṃ yat sarvam āyur eti vasīyān bhavati sarvam āyur eti vasīyān bhavati ya evaṃ veda navarātro vā eṣa nava prāṇāḥ prāṇeṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho bhavati pratyakṣam ṛddhayā atha yat jyotir gaur āyur atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhityai

jyotiṣṭomo agniṣṭhomo gaur ukthya āyur ukthyo abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho viśvajid atirātraḥ paśukāmo yajeta yat jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ purastād bhavati prajñātān stomānupaitīmān eva lokān eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati atha yad abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāho madhyato bhavati pāṅktaḥ purūṣaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavas tena purūṣaṃ ca paśūṃś cāpnoti viśvajid atirātro bhavati viśvasyābhijityai

trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyas trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ saptadaśo agniṣṭoma ekaviṃśa ukthyaḥ saptadaśo agniṣṭomas triṇavo agniṣṭomas trayastriṃśa ukthyas triṇavo agniṣṭomo viśvajid atirātraḥ indro asurān hatvākāryaṃ cakṛvāṃ amanyata taṃ devā etena stomenāyājayan sa pāpmano nairdaśyam agacchat tasmād iṣuhato vā daṇḍahato vā daśamīṃ nairdaśyaṃ gacchati daśa daśinī vā eṣā virāḍ annaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāsmin dadhāti agniṣṭomena vai devā asurān nigṛhya madhyata ukthaiḥ prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyantāgniṣṭomenaiva bhrātṛvyaṃ nigṛhya madhyata ukthyaiḥ prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāyate trikakub vā eṣa yajñaḥ trikakup samānānāṃ ca prajānāṃ ca bhavati ya evaṃ veda trayastrivṛto agniṣṭomās trayaḥ pañcadaśa ukthyās trayaḥ saptadaśa ukthyā ekaviṃśo atirātraḥ kusuruvindadaśarātraḥ yaḥ kāmayeta bahu syām iti sa etena yajeta yad gaṇaśaḥ stomo bahur eva bhavati saha trivṛta saha pañcadaśāḥ saha saptadaśāḥ ekaviṃśo atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhityai jyotir vā eṣa vihṛtaḥ jyotiṣ prajānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda catuṣṭomo vā eṣa catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati ekaviṃśaṃ stomā nātiyanti pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśaḥ praty eva tiṣṭhati etena vai kusurūvinda auddālakir iṣṭvā bhūmānam āśnuta bhūmānam aśnute ya evaṃ veda

abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāhaś catvāraś chandomaḥ viśvajid atirātraḥ paśukāmo yajeta yad abhyāsaṅgyaḥ pañcāhaḥ purastād bhavati pāṅktaḥ puruṣaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavas tena purūṣaṃ ca paśūṃś cāpnoti chandomā madhyato bhavanti paśavo vai chandomāḥ paśūnām avarudhyai viśvajid atirātro bhavati viśvasyābhijityai

triṣṭomo agniṣṭomo jyotir ukthyas triṣṭomo agniṣṭomo gaurukthyo abhijid agniṣṭomo gaur ukthyo viśvajid agniṣṭoma āyur ukthyo viśvajid agniṣṭomasya sarvastomo atirātraḥ devā vā asurair hanyamānās te prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs tebhya etāṃ devapuraṃ prāyacchat tāṃ prāviśan abhicāryamāṇaṃ yājayed etām eva devapuraṃ praviśaty asṛtyai

abhyāsaṅgyaḥ ṣaḍahas trayaś chandomāś catuṣṭomo agniṣṭomo viśvajid atirātraḥ svārājyo vā eṣa yajñaḥ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda prajāpatir hi svārājyaṃ parameṣṭhī svārājyam parameṣṭhitāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavatas tad dhi svārājyam ayutaṃ dakṣiṇās tad dhi svārājyaṃ ṣaḍviṃśastomo bhavati sa hi svārājyaṃ catuṣṭomastomaḥ sa hy anto ante śriyā gacchati ya evaṃ veda etena vai kṣema dhṛtvā pauṇḍarīkaṃ iṣṭvā sudāmnas tīra uttare sarvām ṛddhim ārdhnot sarvāmṛddhim ṛdhnoti ya evaṃ veda

atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ sarvastomo atirātraś catvāraś chandomā atirātraḥ eṣa vā āpto dvādaśāho yat trayodaśarātraḥ samāno hy eṣa yat prayaṇīyaś codayanīyaś cātirātrau kāmaṃ kāmayante tam etābhir abhyaśnuvate gṛhapates tu vāg upadāsukā bhavati tad yan madhye sarvastomo atirātro bhavati tena gṛhapater vāg anupadāsukā bhavati etā vā aryalagṛhapataya ārūṇihotāraḥ subhagāsūpayanti te sarvām ṛddhim ārdhnuvan sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnuvanti ya etā upayanti

atirātro dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca vāg vā eṣā pratāyate yad eṣa dvādaśāhas tāṃ vicchindyur yan madhye atirātraṃ kuryuḥ yad upariṣṭād vratam upayanti na vācaṃ vicchindanty āpnuvanti trayodaśaṃ māsam etā vai pratiṣṭhitās trayodaśa rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇo atirātraḥ kāmasanayo vā etā rātrayaḥ virāḍh ḍhi daśātmaikādaśī prajā dvādaśī paśavas trayodaśī kāmāya caturdaśī sarvān evaitābhiḥ kāmān avarūndhate etā vāva bradhnasya viṣṭapo yad etau trayastriṃśau madhyataḥ saṃdhīyete tena bradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ rohanti dviḥ pṛṣṭhāny upayanty abhipūrvam evaitābhir annādyaṃ dadhate

atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ pṛṣṭhya ṣaḍaha āyur gaur jyotir atirātraḥ yāṃs talpe vodake vā vivāhe vā mīmāṃseraṃs ta etā upeyuḥ yat jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ prajñātāṃ stomān upayanti imān eva lokān eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhānti atha yat pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho madhyato bhavaty eṣu vāva devatalpo devatalpam eva tad ārohanti talpyā bhavanti pravasīyasas talpam āpnuvanti atha yad āyur gaur jyotir atirātro yeneto yanti tena punar āyanti

atirātro gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ yad gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī bhavato mithunau stomāv upayanti prajātyai atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāya etā vai pratiṣṭhitāś caturdaśa rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho mahāvrataṃ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇo atirātraḥ etābhir vai devā devatvam agacchan devatvaṃ gacchanti ya etā upayanti etad vai devānāṃ sattraṃ tad adyāpi devāḥ sattram āsate paurṇamāsy atirātro atha yāni ṣaḍ ahāni sa pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaha ekāṣṭakā mahāvratam atha yāni ṣaḍ ahāni sa pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho amāvāsyātirātraḥ tasmāt tarhi manuṣyāṇāṃ na suto devānāṃ hi tarhi sutaḥ pratyakṣam evaitābhir devatā abhyārohanti pratinodāt tu bhayyam itaram anupakṣo dīkṣerann apratinodāya

atirātras trivṛd agniṣṭud agniṣṭomo jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaha āyur gaur jyotir atirātraḥ kṣatraṃ vā etā rātrayo abhinirvadanti brahmavarcasakāmā upeyuḥ yat trivṛd agniṣṭud agniṣṭomo bhavati brahma tad yaśasārdhayati brahma vai trivṛt yat jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ prajñātān stomān upayantīmān eva lokān eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanty atha yat pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho madhyato bhavaty annaṃ vai pṛṣṭāny annam eva tan madhyato dhīyate tasmān madhye sad annaṃ dhinoty atha yad āyur gaur jyotir atirātro yeneto yanti tena punar āyanti

trivṛd agniṣṭud agniṣṭomo jyotir gaur āyus tryaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ anyasmai vai kāmāya sattram anyasmai yajño na tat sattreṇāpnoti yasmaikaṃ yajño na tad yajñenāpnoti yasmaikaṃ sattram yad anyato atirātrās tena yajño atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni tena sattram ubhāv evaitābhiḥ kāmāv avarūndhate

atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ prajākāmā upeyuḥ etābhir vai prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyante ya etā upayanti yat jyotir gaur āyus tryahaḥ prajātān stomān upayantīmān eva lokān eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāya etā vai pratiṣṭhitāḥ pañcadaśa rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

etā eva samahāvratāḥ etābhir vā indraḥ paramāṃ vijitiṃ vyajayata paramām evaitābhir vijitiṃ vijayante pañcadaśo vai vajro na vā agṛhītena vajreṇa vīryaṃ karoti yā ṣoḍaśy ārambhaṇam eva tad gṛhītena vajreṇa vīryaṃ karoti

atirātro jyotir gaur āyur gaur āyuḥ pañcāho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ etābhir vai prajāpatir anantāṃ śriyam ajayad anantā vā etā yat pañcāhavidhāḥ yat pañcāho anantād eva prajāyante atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāya etā vai pratiṣṭhitāḥ saptadaśa rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

atirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ devā vai mṛtyor abibhayus te prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs tebhya etenāṣṭādaśarātreṇāmṛtatvaṃ prāyacchat etad vāva manuṣyasyāmṛtatvaṃ yat sarvam āyur eti vasīyān bhavati sarvam āyur yanti vasīyāṃso bhavanti ya etā upayanti dvir vā etā nava nava prāṇā abhipūrvam evaitābhir āyur dadhate

etā eva samahāvratāḥ etābhir vai vāyur āraṇyānāṃ paśunām ādhipatyaṃ gacchanti ya etā upayanti mṛgasatraṃ vā etat etābhir vā āraṇyāḥ paśavo nākṛtāḥ prajāyante anākṛtam eṣāṃ prajāyate ya etā upayanti

atrirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho abhijic ca viśvajic ca dve ahanī dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ purūṣakāmā upeyur etābhir vai prajāpatiḥ purūṣam asṛjata sa sarvasyānnādyasyādhipatyam agacchat sarvasyānnādyasyādhipatyaṃ gacchanti ya etā upayanti purūṣasatraṃ vā etat viṃśo vai purūṣo daśa hi hastyā aṅgulyo daśa pādyāḥ yad etā viṃśatī rātrayo bhavanty eṣv evaitābhir lokeṣu purūṣaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayanti etā vai pratiṣṭhitā viṃśatī rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

atirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho atirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho atirātraḥ paśukāmā upeyuḥ etābhir vā ādityāḥ sapta grāmyān paśūn udasṛjanta paśūn evaitābhir utsṛjanti trir vai sapta saptādityāḥ paśava ādityāḥ ādityā asmiṃl loke ṛddhā ādityā amuṣmin paśavo asmin ṛtavo amuṣmin ubhayor anayor lokayor ṛdhnuvanti devaloke ca manuṣyaloke ca ya etā upayanti

atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahas trayaḥ svarasāmāno divākīrtyam ahas trayaḥ svarasāmānaḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇo atirātro brahmavarcasakāmā upeyuḥ svarbhānur vā āsuraḥ sūryaṃ tamasāvidhyat tasmai devāḥ prāyaścittim aicchaṃs ta etā avindaṃs tābhir asmāt tamo apāghnan apa tamo ghnate ya etā upayanti saumāpauṣaṃ paśum upālabhyam ālabheran somo vai brāhmaṇaḥ paśavaḥ pūṣā svām eva tad devatāṃ paśubhir baṃhayante tvacam evākrata manor ṛcaḥ sāmidhenyo bhavanti manur vai yat kiṃ cāvadat tad bheṣajaṃ bheṣajatāyai naidādhīya upeyuḥ tad dhy eṣa prati tejiṣṭhaṃ tapati kilāsatvāt tu bhayam ati hy ebhyo apahanti etā vā ugradevo rājanir upait sa kilāso abhavat akilāso bhavati ya evaṃ vidvānetā upaiti

atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryaho abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś cānnādyakāmā upeyuḥ pañcartavo dvādaśa māsās traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśo annaṃ dvāviṃśam ebhyo lokebhyaḥ saṃvatsarād amuṣmād ādityād annādyam avarundhate ya etā upayanti

atirātro jyotir gaur āyur gaur āyuḥ pañcāho abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ pratiṣṭhākāmā upeyuḥ etābhir vai prajāpatir eṣu lokeṣu pratyatiṣṭhat yad etās trayoviṃśatī rātrayo bhavanti traya ime lokā eṣv evaitābhir lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti etā vai pratiṣṭhitās trayoviṃśatī rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ stomaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśam ahar aniruktam upahavyasya tantre kḷpta tasya kaṇvarathantaraṃ madhyandine atha trayastriṃśa niruktaṃ triṇavaṃ dve ekaviṃśe triṇavaṃ trayastriṃśam ahar niruktaṃ trayastriṃśam ahar aniruktam pṛṣṭhayaḥ stomaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ pratyaṅ trivṛd ahar aniruktaṃ jyotiṣṭomo agniṣṭomo atirātraḥ etābhir vai devāḥ svarge loke samasīdan svarge loke sīdāmety etāḥ etā vāva bradhnasya viṣṭapo yad ete trayastiṃśā madhyataḥ saṃdhīyante tena bradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ rohanti madhyataḥ pṛṣṭhāny upayanty annaṃ vai pṛṣṭhāny annam eva tan madhyato dhīyate tasmān madhye sad annaṃ dhinoti saptāhā vā ete ato vai prajāḥ prajāyante pra prajayā pra paśubhirjāyante ya etā upayanti apaśavyaṃ vā etat sattraṃ yad acchandomaṃ yat saptāhās tena chandomavatyas tena paśavyāḥ trayastriṃśas trayastriṃśam anveti trivṛt trivṛtam agrād agraṃ rohanti yat trayastriṃśas trayastriṃśam anveti prāṇāt prāṇeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti yat trivṛt trivṛtam vilomāno vā etā rātrayo yat jyotir agniṣṭoma utthānīyam ahar bhavaty akḷptasya kḷptyai

atirātro dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ prajākāmā vā paśukāmā vopeyuḥ kḷptādvai yoneḥ prajāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante yat kḷptau ṣaḍahāv upayanti kḷptādeva yoneḥ prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāyante atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāya etā vai pratiṣṭhitāś caturviṃśatī rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti

etā eva samahāvratāḥ etābhir vai prajāpatiḥ sarvam annādyam avārūndha caturviṃśatiḥ saṃvatsarasyārdhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ pañcaviṃśo annaṃ vrataṃ saṃvatsarād etābhir annādyam avarūndhate ya etā upayanti

atirātro gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍāhau dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ ṛtavo na pratyatiṣṭhaṃs ta etābhiḥ pratyatiṣṭhan pratiṣṭhākāmā upeyuḥ praty eva tiṣṭhanti ṣaḍ vā ṛtava ṛtuṣv evaitābhiḥ pratitiṣṭhanti yad gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī bhavato mithunau stomāv upayanti prajātyai yat kḷptau ṣaḍahāv upayanti kḷptyā eva atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāya etā vai pratiṣṭhitā ṣaḍviṃśatī rātrayaḥ pratitiṣṭhanti ya etā upayanti atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryaho dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātra ṛddhikāmā upeyuḥ etābhir vai nakṣatrāṇi sarvāmṛddhim ārdhnuvan sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnuvanti ya etā upayanti yad etā saptaviṃśatī rātrayo bhavanti saptaviṃśatir nakṣatrāṇi nakṣatrasammitā vā etā rātrayo nakṣatrāṇām evardhim ṛdhnuvanti

etā eva samahāvratāḥ paśukāmā upeyur yad etā aṣṭāviṃśatī rātrayo bhavanty aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśa evaitābhiḥ paśūn avarūndhate

atirātro jyotir gaur āyur gaur āyuḥ pañcāho dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ etābhir vai prajāpatir anantāṃ śriyam ajayat anantā vā etā yā ekayānatriṃśann eti vai vāco anantam yad etā ekayānatriṃśad rātrayo bhavanty anantām evaitābhiḥ śriyaṃ jayanti

atirātras trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātro annādyakāmā upeyuḥ parokṣam anyāni sattrāṇi virājaṃ sampadyante pratyakṣam etā virājaṃ sampannāḥ pratyakṣam etābhir annādyam avarūndhate ya etā upayanti

etā eva samahāvratā etābhir vai prajāpatir abhipūrvam annādyam avārūndha annaṃ virāḍ annaṃ vratam abhipūrvam evaitābhir annādyam avarūndhate

atirātro gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ paśukāmā upeyuḥ anuṣṭub vā etā rātrayaḥ dvātriṃśad akṣarānuṣṭup vāg anuṣṭup catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ vācā paśūn dādhāra etābhī rātrībhiḥ tasmāt te vācā siddhā vācāhūtā ā yanti

atirātras trayaḥ pañcāhā viśvajid atirātra ekaḥ pañcāho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā na pratyatiṣṭhaṃs tā etābhiḥ pratyatiṣṭhann ime lokā na pratyatiṣṭhaṃs ta etābhiḥ pratyatiṣṭhan pratyatiṣṭhan pratiṣṭhākāmā upeyuḥ praty eva tiṣṭhanti arūpeṇa vā etāḥ sarūpā arūpeṇa prajāḥ sarūpā arūpeṇeme lokāḥ sarūpā yad rathantarasya lokaṃ bṛhad āpadyate bṛhato rathantaram arūpeṇaivaibhyas tat sarūpaṃ prajanayanti lupyate vā etat ṣaṣṭham ahar yat pañcāhān upayanti nartavaḥ kalpanteḥ yat pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍahas tena ṣaṣṭham ahar na lupyate tenartavaḥ kalpante atha yāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni tena pañcāhebhyo na yanti ūdhar vā antarikṣaṃ stanāv abhito anena vā eṣa devebhyo dugdhe amunā prajābhyaḥ idaṃ vā antarikṣaṃ viyad imau stanāv abhitaḥ tad abhyanūktā triṃśati trayaḥ paro ye devā barhir āsata vyann aha dvitā taneti ūdhar vai madhyamo atirātraḥ stanāv abhitaḥ yad eṣo anatirātraḥ syād ūdhaḥ pratiharet tasmād atirātraḥ kārya ūdhaso apratihārāya trayastriṃśad devatā etābhir ārdhnuvaṃs tenardhis tasmād etābhir yajanta ṛdhyā eva nānā brahmasāmāny upayanty ahnā nānā vīryatāyai nānaiva vīryāṇy avarūndhate

atirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho atirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho atirātro abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirāś ca ādityāś cāṅgirasaś caitat sattraṃ samadadhatādityānām ekaviṃśatir aṅgirasāṃ dvādaśāha ādityā asmiṃl loka ṛddhā ādityā amuṣminn aṅgiraso asminn aṅgiraso amuṣmin dvayaṃ sattraṃ yāvad dvayena sattreṇardhnuvanti tāvaty etāsām ṛddhiḥ

atirātras trayaḥ pañcāhā viśvajid atirātras trayaḥ pañcāhā atirātraḥ apaśavyaṃ vā etat sattraṃ yad acchandomaṃ yadviśvajiti chandomān upayanti tena chandomavatyas tena paśavyāḥ pakṣiṇyo vā etā rātrayo yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayante tam etābhir abhyaśnuvate yatra yatra hi pakṣī kāmayate tat tad abhyaśnute trivṛtā prayanti trivṛtodyanti prāṇā vai trivṛt stomānāṃ prāṇair eva prayanti prāṇeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti

atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryahas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś cardhikāmā upeyuḥ etābhir vai prajāpatiḥ sarvām ṛddhim ārdhnot sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnuvanti ya etā upayanti yad etāś catustriṃśad rātrayo bhavanti trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpater evardhim ṛdhnuvanti atirātro jyotir gaur āyuḥ pañcāhas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ paśukāmā upeyuḥ yad etāḥ pañcātriṃśad rātrayo bhavanti pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ paśūn evaitābhir avarundhate

atirātraś catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ paśukāmā upeyuḥ etābhir vai devā ādityam astabhnuvann ādityalokaṃ jayanti ya etā upayanti bṛhatī vā etā rātrayaḥ svārājyaṃ chandasāṃ bṛhatī yo vai paśūnāṃ bhūmānaṃ gacchati sa svārājyaṃ gacchati pra svārājyam āpnuvanti ya etā upayanti

etā eva samahāvratāḥ etābhir vai prajāpatir ubhau kāmāv avārūndhānnaṃ vrataṃ paśavo bṛhaty ubhāv evaitābhiḥ kāmāv avarūndhate

atirātro gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ paśukāmā upeyuḥ spaṣṭo arthaḥ yad etā aṣṭātriṃśad rātrayo bhavanty aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśa evaitābhiḥ paśun avarūndhate

atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryahaś catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ etābhir vai prajāpatir anantā śriyam ajayad anantā vā etā yā ekayānacatvāriṃśan neti vai vāco anantam yad etā ekayānacatvāriṃśad rātrayo bhavanty anantām evaitābhiḥ śriyaṃ jayanti

etā eva samahāvratāḥ sarvā vā etā virājo daśinī prathamā viṃśinī dvitīyā triṃśinī tṛtīyaiṣā vai paramā virāṭ yac catvāriṃśad rātrayaḥ paṅktir vai paramā virāṭ paramāyām eva virāji pratitiṣṭhanti

atirātras trīṇi trivṛnty ahāny agniṣṭomamukhāny atirātro daśa pañcadaśā ukthyāḥ ṣoḍaśimad daśamam ahar atirātro dvādaśa saptadaśā ukthyā atirātraḥ pṛṣṭhayaḥ ṣaḍaho atirātro dvādaśaikaviṃśā ukthyā atirātraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā avidhṛtā asañjānānā anyonyām ādaṃs tena prajāpatir aśocat sa etā apaśyat tato vā idaṃ vyāvartata gāvo abhavann aśvā aśvāḥ purūṣāḥ purūṣā mṛgā mṛgāḥ vi pāpmanā vartante ya etā upayanti yad atirātrā antarā vidhṛtyai tasmān netara itarasmin reto dadhāti yat pṛṣṭhyāḥ stomāḥ sa sṛṣṭās tasmād ajāvayaḥ paśūnāṃ saha caranti tasmād u gardabho vaḍavāyā reto dadhāti apaśavyaṃ vā etat sattraṃ yad acchandomaṃ yat sandhiṣāmasu chandāṃsy upayanti tena chandomavatyas tena paśavyāḥ gāyatrīṣu jarābodhīyam uṣṇikṣu śrudhyam anuṣṭupsu nānadaṃ bṛhatīṣu rathantaraṃ paṅktiṣu rāyovājīyaṃ triṣṭupsv auśanaṃ jagatīṣu kāvam ūrdhvāni chandāṃsy upayanty anapabhraṃśāya prāṇo vai svaro yat svarāv antato bhavatas tasmāt dvāv antataḥ prāṇau

atirātrau dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau gauś cāyuś cātirātrau dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahāv abhijic ca viśvajic catirātrāv eko abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ sarvastomaś ca nava saptadaśaś cātirātro dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca ādityānāṃ yamātirātrāḥ yamevaiṣā śrīr bhavati ya etā upayanti etābhir vā ādityā dvandvam ārdhnuvan mitraś ca varūṇaś ca dhātā cāryamā cāṃśaś ca bhagaś cendraś ca vivasvāś caitāsām eva devatānām ṛddhim ṛdhnuvanti ya etā upayanti tad abhyanūktā aṣṭau putrāso aditer ye jātās tanvaṃ pari devā upaprait saptabhiḥ parā mārtāṇḍam āsyad iti ādityā asmiṃl loka ṛddhā ādityā amuṣminn ubhayor anayor lokayor ṛdhnuvanti devaloke ca manuṣyaloke ca ya etā upayanti atirātraś catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ sarvastomo atirātro dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa rūkṣo abhavat taṃ rūkṣaṃ nājanan sa ā cāṅktābhi cāṅkta ya ātmānaṃ neva jānīraṃs ta etā upeyur yadā cāñjate abhi cāñjate śubham evātman dadhate jānanty enān gauggulavena prātassavane saugandhikena mādhyandine savane paitudāraveṇa tṛtīyasavane agnir vai devānāṃ hautram upaiṣyañ charīram adhūnuta tasya yanmāṃ samāsīt tad guggulv abhavadyat snāva tat sugandhitejanaṃ yad asthi tat potudārv etāni vai devasurabhīṇi devasurabhibhir eva tad abhyañjate

atirātraś caturviṃśaṃ prāyaṇīyam ahas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā abhijit trayaḥ svarasāmāno divākīrtyam ahas trayaḥ svarasāmāno viśvajid eko abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaha āyuś ca gauś ca dve āhanī dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca saṃvatsarasam mitā yāvatī saṃvatsarasyarddhis tāvaty etāsām ṛddhiḥ tad āhur yac caturviṃśam ahaḥ prayaṇīyaṃ kuryuḥ saṃvatsaram ārabhya na samāpayeyur iti trivṛd eva kāryaṃ prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān evopayanti atho khalv āhuś caturviṃśam eva kāryaṃ samṛdhyai athaite svarasāmānaḥ śiro vai divākīrtyaṃ prāṇāḥ svarasāmāno yad divākīrtyam abhitaḥ svarasāmāno bhavanti śirasyeva tat prāṇā dhīyante atha yāvantyau prāṇau tau viśvajid abhijitāv athaite goāyuṣī mithunau stomāv upayanti prajātyai athaitāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāya athaitad vratam annaṃ vai vrata na vā anyatra mukhād annaṃ dhinoti yad upariṣṭād vratam upayanti mukhata eva tad annādyaṃ dhīyate tasmān mukhe sad annaṃ dhinoti athaitau prāyaṇīyodayanīyāv atirātrau yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudhanti

atirātro nava trivṛnty ahāny agniṣṭomamukhaṣ ṣaḍaho atha yāni trīṇy ahāny agniṣṭomāv abhita ukthyaṃ madhyato nava pañcadaśāny ahāny agniṣṭomam ukhaḥ ṣaḍaho atha yāni trīṇy ahāny agniṣṭomāv abhita ukthyaṃ madhyato nava saptadaśāny ahāny agniṣṭomamukhaḥ ṣaḍaho atha yāni trīṇy ahāny agniṣṭomāv abhita ukthyaṃ madhyato navaikaviṃśāny ahāny agniṣṭomamukhaḥ ṣaḍaho atha yāni trīṇy ahāny agniṣṭomāv abhita ukthyaṃ madhyato dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca etābhir vai savitā sarvasya prasavam agacchat sarvasya prasavaṃ gacchanti ya etā upayanti yad gaṇaśaḥ stomā bahava eva bhavanti saha trivṛtaḥ saha pañcadaśāḥ saha saptadaśāḥ sahaikaviṃśāḥ savitur vā etāḥ kakubhaḥ kakubhaḥ samānānāṃ ca prajānāṃ ca bhavanti ya etā upayanti

atirātraś catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā mahāvrataṃ dvāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau dvādaśāhasya daśāhāny atirātraḥ ṛtavo na pratyatiṣṭhaṃs ta etābhiḥ pratyatiṣṭhan pratiṣṭhākāmā upeyuḥ praty eva tiṣṭhanti ṣaḍ vā ṛtava ṛtuṣv evaitābhiḥ pratitiṣṭhanti yat kḷptān ṣaḍahān upayanti kḷptyā eva athaitad vratam annaṃ vai vrataṃ na vā anyatra madhyād annaṃ dhinoti yad vrataṃ madhyata upayanti madhyata eva tad annādyaṃ dhīyate tasmān madhye sad annaṃ dhinoti yat kḷptau ṣaḍahāv upayanti kḷptyā eva athaitāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāyāthaitau prāyaṇīyodayanīyāv atirātrau yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti

atirātraḥ ṣaḍabhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca etābhir vā indrāgnī atyanyā devatā abhavatām atyanyāḥ prajā bhavanti ya etā upayanti indrāgnī vai devānām ojiṣṭhā ojiṣṭhā bhavanti ya etā upayanti yat kḷptān ṣaḍahān upayanti kḷptyā evāthaitāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vācam avicchinnām upayanti prajananāyāthaitad vratam athaitau prāyaṇīyodayanīyāv atirātrau yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudhanti

atirātraś caturviṃśaṃ prāyaṇīyam ahas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho abhijit trayassvarasāmāno divākīrtyam ahas trayaḥ svarasāmāno viśvajit pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇa eko abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaha āyuś ca gauś ca dve ahanī dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataś cātirātraś ca tad etad ekaṣaṣṭirātraṃ daivānāṃ vrātyānām daivā vai vrātyāḥ sattram āsata budhena sthapatinā te ha vā aniryācya varuṇaṃ rājānaṃ devayajanaṃ didīkṣus tān ha vā varūṇo rājānu vyājahārāntar emi vo yajñiyād bhāgadheyān na devayānaṃ panthānaṃ prajñāsyatheti tasmāt tebhyo na havir gṛhṇanti na graham atha ha vai tarhi nauṣadhīṣu paya āsīn na kṣīre sarpir na māṃse medo na tvaci lomāni na vanaspatiṣu palāśāni tad yata etad ekaṣaṣṭirātraṃ daivā vrātyā upāyaṃs tato vai tāni bhutāny etair vīryaiḥ samasṛjyanta tejasvanty evāsan payasvanti tad eṣa śloko abhyanūcyate kim akarteti yat putrān muhur daivāṃ apṛcchata mahī budhasyāsīd dīkṣā sa kṣīre sarpir āharat mahīṃ dīkṣāṃ saumāyano budho yad udayacchadanandat sarvam āpnon manmāṃse medo adhā iti daridrā āsan paśavaḥ kṛśāḥ santo vyasthakāḥ saumāyanasya dīkṣāyāṃ samasṛjyanta medaseti tad ya etad ekaṣaṣṭirātram upeyus te devayajanam adhyavasāya gārhapatya āhutiṃ juhayur deva varuṇa devayajanaṃ no dehi svāheti te datte devajane yajante te sarvām ṛddhim ārdhnuvan sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnuvanti ya etad upayanti

atirātro jyotir gaur āyus tryahaś caturdaśābhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca devā vai mṛtyor abibhayus te prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs tebhya etena śatarātreṇāmṛtatvaṃ prāyacchad etad vāva manuṣyasyāmṛtatvaṃ yat sarvam āyur eti vasīyān bhavati sarvam āyur yanti vasīyāṃso bhavanti ya etad upayanti abhiprayāyam abhiṣuṇvanty abhikrāntyai samānatrābhiṣuṇvanti pratiṣṭhityai

atirātraś caturviṃśaṃ prāyaṇīyam ahaś catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ sa māsaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ sa caturthaḥ sa pañcamas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho abhijit trayaḥ svarasāmāno divākīrtyam ahas trayaḥ svarasāmāno viśvajit pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇaś catvāro abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ sa māsaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ sa caturthas trayo abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahā āyuś ca gauś ca dve ahanī dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni mahāvrañcātirātraś ca saṃvatsarabrāhmaṇaṃ brāhmaṇam

atirātraś caturviṃśaṃ prāyaṇīyam ahar dvau trivṛt pañcadaśau ṣaḍahau pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho dvau trivṛt pañcadaśau ṣaḍahau sa māsaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ sa caturthaḥ sa pañcamas trayas trivṛt pañcadaśāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahas trivṛd bṛhaspatistomas trayaḥ svarasāmāno divākīrtyam ahas trayaḥ svarasāmānaḥ pañcadaśa indrastoma ukthyaḥ pṛṣṭyaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇa ekaḥ pañcadaśas trivṛt ṣaḍaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vyūḍhā agniṣṭomās trivṛta udbhic ca balabhic ca dve ahanī dvau pañcadaśatrivṛtau ṣaḍahau pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho dvau pañcadaśatribṛtau ṣaḍahau sa māsaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ sa caturthaḥ pañcadaśatrivṛt ṣaḍahaḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaḥ pañcadaśatrivṛt ṣaḍaho gauś cāyuś ca dve ahanī chandomadaśāho aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ prathamam ahar atha catuścatvāriṃśaṃ catvāriṃśaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaṃ dvātriṃśaṃ triṃśaṃ dve aṣṭāviṃśe pañcaviṃśaṃ caturviṃśaṃ mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś ca ādityānām madhye pṛṣṭhyam madhye pṛṣṭhyena vā ādityāḥ svargaṃ lokam ākramanta yan madhye pṛṣṭhāny upayanti svargasya lokasyākrāntyai annaṃ vai pṛṣṭhāny annam eva tan madhyato dhīyate tasmān madhye sad annaṃ dhinoti paśavaḥ pṛṣṭhāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanti cakre vā ete sākaṃvṛtīyat trivṛt pañcadaśau stomau yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayante tam etenābhyaśnuvate yatra yatra hi cakrīvatā kāmayate tat tad abhyaśnute athaiṣa trivṛd bṛhaspatistoma etena vai bṛhaspatir devānāṃ purodhām agacchat purodhakāmā upeyur gacchanti purodhāṃ pura enān dadhate athaite svarasāmānaḥ śiro vai divākīrtyaṃ prāṇāḥ svarasāmāno yad divākīrtyam abhitaḥ svarasāmāno bhavanti śivasyeva tat prāṇā dhīyante athaiṣa pañcadaśa indrastoma ukthya etena vā indro atyanyā devatā abhavad atyanyāḥ prajā bhavanti ya etad upayanti athaitāni dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vyūḍhā agniṣṭomās trivṛto madhyataḥ pāpmano mucyanta eṣa vāva devatalpo devatalpam eva tad ārohanti talpyā bhavanti pravasīyasas talpam āpnuvanti athaitāv udbhidbalabhidāv etābhyāṃ vai bṛhaspatir devebhyaḥ paśūn udasṛjat paśūn evaitābhyām utsṛjante athaite go āyuṣī mithunau stomāv upayanti prajātyai athaiṣa chandomadaśāhaś chandasāṃ doho arvāñci chandāṃsy upayanti tasmād arvāñco bhuñjantaḥ paśava upatiṣṭhante athaid vratam annaṃ vai vrataṃ na vā anyatra mukhād annaṃ dhinoti yad upariṣṭād vratam upayanti mukhata eva tad annādyaṃ dhīyate tasmān mukhe sad annaṃ dhinoti athaitau prāyaṇīyodayanīyāv atirātrau yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti

atirātraś caturviṃśaṃ prāyaṇīyam ahaḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaś catvāras trivṛto abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ sa māsaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ sa caturthaḥ sa pañcamas trayas trivṛto abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahas trivṛd bṛhaspatistomas trayaḥ svarasāmāno divākīrtyam ahas trayaḥ svarasāmānaḥ pañcadaśa indrastoma ukthyaḥ pṛṣṭyaḥ ṣaḍahas trayastriṃśārambhaṇa ekas trivṛd abhiplavaḥ ṣaḍaho dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni vyūḍhā agniṣṭomās trivṛta udbhic ca balabhic ca dve ahanī catvāras trivṛto abhiplavāḥ ṣaḍahāḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahau sa māsaḥ sa dvitīyaḥ sa tṛtīyaḥ sa caturtho dvau trivṛtāv abhiplavau ṣaḍahau pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaha āyuś ca gauś ca dve ahanī chandomadaśāhaś caturviṃśaṃ prathamam ahar dve aṣṭāviṃśe triṃśaṃ dvātriṃśaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaṃ catvāriṃśaṃ catuścatvāriṃśam aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ caturviṃśaṃ mahāvrataṃ cātirātraś cāṅgirasāṃ purastāt pṛṣṭhyam purastāt pṛṣṭhyena vā aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam ākramanta yat purastāt pṛṣṭhāny upayanti svargasya lokasyākrāntyai annaṃ vai pṛṣṭhāny annam eva tan mukhato dhīyate tasmān mukhe sad annaṃ dhinoti paśavaḥ pṛṣṭhāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanti yad anyac cakrābhyāṃ sākavṛdbhyāṃ tatsamānam ā chandomadaśāhāt athaiṣa chandomadaśāhaś chandasāṃ doha ūrdhvāni chandāṃsy upayanty anapabhraṃśāyaiṣa vāva devayānaḥ panthāḥ pra devayānaṃ panthānam āpnuvanti ya etad upayanty athaitad vratam athaitau prāyaṇīyodayanīyāv atirātrau yenaiṣa prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
